Part of the combat encounter guarding the portal to the Shadowfell.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |

Flies past without attacking.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |

Pose a threat to anyone trying to reach the floating fortress.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| Soul Armor Guardian                       | S02E22                         | A massive chain-powered construct guarding the throne room/vault on the sixth floor of Zentil Keep. Animated by the soul engine's energy, it uses chain attacks and area effects. Defeated by SWOJ in a fierce battle, with Scoot landing critical blows.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
| Otyugh                                    | S02E23                         | A refuse-eating aberration inhabiting the trash room beneath Zentil Keep. Xae communicates with it using speak with animals. The party collects its stench for tactical use.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| Flesh Golems                              | S02E23                         | Hulking golems made of flesh and metal, found sealed in coffin-like containers in the underground tunnels. Bound by iron clasps as if sleeping. Created by Friar Truck for Rowan Crooks' forces.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| Rowan Crooks Clones                       | S02E24                         | Clones of Rowan Crooks (Manshoon) found in various stages of development in Friar Truck's clone tanks. Destroyed by Scoot before they could reach maturity.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |
| Giant Constrictor Snakes                  | S02E24                         | Summoned by Xae via conjure animals during the sky-falling battle. Two giant snakes that wrap around Crooks' arms and legs to restrain him. One successfully grapples his legs. Crooks escapes via misty step.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
| Shadow Swoj                               | S02E25                         | Dark reflections of each party member that appear as the final challenge in the Raven Queen's dream sequence. Each shadow version mirrors the abilities and fighting style of the original party member.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
| Bulettes                                  | S02E26                         | Massive burrowing creatures also known as 'land sharks.' Attack SWOJ on the High Road south of Neverwinter. Emerge from underground to ambush travelers. Were attracted by the scent of Lachlina's Lunaria herbs.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| Shaleheart                                | S02E26                         | A domesticated or friendly bulette that joins SWOJ as an ally during the bulette encounter on the High Road. Unlike the wild bulettes, Shaleheart is cooperative and becomes a companion.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
| Will-O'-Wisps                             | S02E27                         | Floating orbs of spectral light encountered in the Mere of Dead Men. Attempt to lure travelers off safe paths to their doom in the swamp. A classic swamp hazard.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| Otyughs (Baby)                            | S02E27                         | Tentacled aberrations that hatch from eggs found in the ruined wizard tower at Castle Naerytar. Approximately 20 eggs hatch simultaneously. Have three tentacles with barbed tips, a gaping angler-fish-like mouth, and small legs. Eat garbage and refuse. Xae befriends one through animal handling, and the entire brood follows her. Similar to the larger otyugh encountered at Zentil Keep. The mother otyugh was killed by the cultists.                                                                                                |
| Cult Of The Dragon Guards                 | S02E27                         | Humanoid cultists wearing black dragon masks who guard Castle Naerytar. Five patrol the outer walls, approximately 25-30 more operate inside performing excavation and other tasks.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| Otyughs                                   | S02E28                         | Swamp monsters native to the Mere of Dead Men. SWOJ uses twenty freshly hatched baby otyughs as a distraction force against the cultists.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
| Saboteur Agents                           | S02E30                         | Three infiltrators who attack Castle Never: a wizard in a hooded robe, a knife-wielding secret agent decked with tools, and a shadow assassin who moved invisibly. They bomb the Ethereal Galleon at the dry docks and attempt to steal Wren's soul stone. Lark kills the shadow assassin, but the wizard and knife agent escape via dimension door.                                                                                                                                                                                           |
| Barbarian Periton Riders                  | S02E32                         | Fierce warriors covered in war paint who ride peritons. Connected to Malar the Beast Lord. Armed with weighted nets, crowbars, and explosives. They board ships during combat and chant in coordination with the peritons' song. Intimidated by Scoot's deception about ethereal plane-shifting.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| Dracolich (Half-Formed)                   | S02E33                         | A massive half-formed skeletal dragon circling the Radiant Citadel. Has two improperly merged heads from the ritual that created it -- two dragon twin skeletal bases poke from the neck. Larger than when last seen and still growing. Arrived just days ago and terrorizes the city, destroying buildings and capturing people. Enters the Preserve of Ancestors to capture the dragon incarnate in an orb of force. Mostly hangs near the top of the citadel.                                                                               |
| Soul-Crystal Guards                       | S02E33                         | Two heavily armored warriors guarding Melifarn's body in the Preserve of Ancestors. Enhanced with soul crystals embedded in their armor: one with golden crystals projecting a spectral lion head (triggers frightening roar when crystal removed), one with green crystals projecting a spectral crocodile head (releases poison explosion on death). Highly durable -- absorbing 50+ damage while remaining functional. The lion guard eventually flees in terror and renounces his ways.                                                  |
| Two-Headed Dracolich                      | S02E34                         | A massive undead dragon with two heads, empowered by the Dawn Incarnate crystals. It guards the top of the Citadel. Banished by divine intervention from the Raven Queen when Scoot communes with her.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |
| Giant Crawfish (Old Salty)                | S02E34                         | An enormous crawfish living in the storm sewers beneath the Citadel. Originally a regular crawfish from Sid's Squids restaurant that was flushed and grew to massive size. Fought and defeated by SWOJ in the sewers.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |

| Crystal-Hearted Specters                  | S02E36                         | Necrotic spectral beings sent by Manshoon's forces in a green wave to attack the party at the Wall of the Faithless. They have glowing soul crystals embedded in their chests that power them. Xae's conjured woodpeckers shatter the crystals to destroy them.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |
| Bone Colossus                             | S02E36                         | A massive undead construct animated from a portion of Kelemvor's skeleton by necrotic energy during the battle at the Wall of the Faithless. It attacks the party. Scoot is hurled at it and uses thunderwave to blast it apart.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| Giant Frog Creatures                      | S02E37                         | At least 10-foot tall frog-like beings from beyond the Wall of the Faithless. They created illusions of SWOJ (Bizarro SWOJ) to lure refugees. Two variants appeared: a green one wielding a wand and a gray one. They have regeneration abilities, telepathic communication (heard as grumbling), and their claws inflict a curse that implants tadpole-like parasites. The gray one escaped through a rift in space. Red in color as tadpoles.                                                                                                |
| Ancient Red Dragon                        | S02E37                         | A massive ancient red dragon spotted in the The Bag Dimension, perched on several bags a couple hundred feet away. It began to turn toward the party and prepare fire breath before they escaped.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
| Frog Creature Tadpoles                    | S02E38                         | Four small red wriggling tadpole-like parasites that grew inside Scoot's wounds from the frog creature claws. Caused fever, reopening wounds, and a magical curse. Removed by Oranax via Remove Curse spell. If allowed to progress, victims may transform into frog creatures or the parasites may burst from their chest. Other refugees on different caravans are also infected.                                                                                                                                                            |
| The Far Realm Creatures                       | S02E38                         | Strange geometric shapes, frog creatures, tentacle beings, and other chaotic entities emerging from portals opening across the Sword Coast. Believed to originate from the Far Realms, released by the breaking of the Wall of the Faithless.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
